url: "https://ammaspastries.in/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",

},

}
});
}
});

Our collective love for sweet indulgence led us to establish a magical realm of divine delicacies that fulfills your utmost desires.</p><p>Now, our reach goes even beyond borders, as we spread our delectable offerings to the enchanting locales of Sharjah (Al Majaz, Al Nahda) ,Dubai (Al Karama, Al Fahidi). &amp; INDIA</p><p>Our mission remains constantto exemplify exceptional customer service and delight you with our premier cakes and pastries. <div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-large">FAQs Related To Amma's Pastries Online Cake <br> Delivery </h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-43722530 elementor-hidden-tablet elementor-hidden-mobile elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="43722530" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h5><strong>Can I Send A Message Or Wish Along With A Cake?</strong></h5>
<ul>
Of course you can. Amma&#8217;s Pastries  provides facility of sending personalized messages along with Cake. While placing an order for cake, you get an option of typing your message in a message box.
</ul>
<h5><strong>Do You Take The Same Day Orders As Well?</strong></h5>
<ul>
Yes, being the best cake shop we do take same-day orders as well, but you need to make them before 10 P.M.
</ul>
<h5><strong>Am I Assured Of Timely Delivery Of The Cake?</strong></h5>
<ul>
We always try our best to deliver cakes on-time and we also make promise for that. But, in some predicaments there might be a slight delay. Although, we will inform our customers in such cases.
</ul>
<h5><strong>Do You Have Any Add-Ons With The Birthday Cakes?</strong></h5>
<ul>
Yes, we have a variety of add on options; Candels , Ballons , Sparkels ..Etc
</ul>
<h5><strong>What Is The Process Of Refund If I Want To Cancel My Order?</strong></h5>
<ul>
Visit &#8211; Our Refund Policy Page <a href="https://ammaspastries.in/terms-condition/">Here</a> to read our <a href="https://ammaspastries.in/terms-condition/">cancellation and refund policy</a>.
</ul> </div>
</div>
